Summary:
A list of factories, outsourcers, hardware components for $40 to $600 Google phones. Unlocked bootloaders are compatible with 10,000 free Linux apps. 

$600 #3 nano Qualcomm Snapdragon 8 Elite Gen5, 6.5" OLED. 
#2 nano thin 2027, #1.6 nano 2028, #1.4 nano 2029, #1.2 nano 2030, #0.2 nano in 2040. 
$10 billion factories 
TaiwanSMC, Intel, Samsung, Rapidus, Tesla Terafab. 
$1,000 microLED folding screens are the best quality, but not sold in phones until 2035.

1 billion more $55 Raspberry Pi5 to $65 Google Go phones TCL Alcatel 1B. 
Taiwan MediaTek MT6580 slow #28 nano meter, RiscV, ARM Cortex C1-Nano. $200 Samsung Galaxy A17 5G is average.

Free TV app Kodi, AV1 compression HandBrake. Vulkan game language Nintendo Dolphin, Lemuroid, M64plusFZ ROM. GameNative Windows games on Google (W.I.N.E. or Winlator.) (XWayland on Android is LocalDesktop.)

Solid state graphene battery 2028. Gallium Nitride electric cables. Solar perovskite, LED red blue chore bots. Filter ocean saltwater in deserts.

Chip designs, "Front-End, which involves designing microarchitecture specifications and describing the logic using Hardware Description Languages (HDLs) like Verilog. (the resulting “code” is called Register Transfer Language, or RTL.) Back-End, which involves taking the RTL, and converting it into a layout (called GDS) that a foundry can use to manufacture the chip. This is a multi-step process that uses EDA tools from companies like Cadence and Synopsys." https://chipinsights.substack.com/p/the-era-of-full-stack-chip-designers

How does memory work? "Each NAND flash cell is essentially a modified transistor, specifically a MOSFET (metal-oxide-semiconductor field-effect transistor) with an additional “floating gate” or, in modern 3D NAND, a charge trap layer. This isolated structure is sandwiched between insulating layers of oxide, allowing it to trap and retain electrical charge (electrons) even when power is off." https://cubiclenate.com/2026/03/04/data-has-weight-but-only-on-ssds-blathering/

"Tesla, Figure, and Apptronik focused on building high-payload general-purpose humanoids, they independently arrived at the same actuator architecture. The constraints of human-like strength and endurance force designers toward a strategic split: rotary actuators for joints that primarily spin, and linear actuators for joints that must absorb heavy shock loads and lift significant weight." "complex gearboxes to convert rotation to linear motion,...artificial muscles...HASEL Actuators (Hydraulically Amplified Self-Healing Electrostatic)...Pneumatic Artificial Muscles (McKibben Muscles)...Twisted String Actuators (TSA)...Dielectric Elastomer Actuators...Shape Memory Alloys (SMA)" https://www.firgelli.com/pages/humanoid-robot-actuators#section-3
